         </ul> </td> 
       </tr> 
      </tbody>
     </table> 
     <p>The university is accredited by the <a href="/wiki/Middle_States_Association_of_Colleges_and_Schools" title="Middle States Association of Colleges and Schools">Middle States Association of Colleges and Schools</a>.</p> 
     <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Academics">Academics</span><span class="mw-editsection">[<a href="/w/index.php?title=University_of_Pittsburgh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Academics">edit</a>]</span></h2> 
     <p>Throughout its history, Pitt has been committed to a liberal arts education with a well-rounded curriculum in the arts, sciences, and humanities.<sup id="cite_ref-Alberts17_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Alberts17-33"><span>[</span>33<span>]</span></a></sup> Pitt has an increasing emphasis on undergraduate research experience and for providing real-world opportunities such as co-ops and internships.<sup id="cite_ref-undergrad-research_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-undergrad-research-82"><span>[</span>82<span>]</span></a></sup> Undergraduate degrees can be earned as Bachelor's of Arts, Bachelor's of Science, and Bachelor's of Philosophy. Along with providing certificate programs, graduate level masters, professional, and doctoral degrees are also awarded. Pitt has also initiated a University-wide Outside the Classroom Curriculum (OCC) that includes a structured series of extracurricular programs and experiences designed to complement students' academic studies and help develop personal attributes and professional skills.<sup id="cite_ref-Outside_the_Classroom_Curriculum:_Your_Pitt_Pathway_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Outside_the_Classroom_Curriculum:_Your_Pitt_Pathway-83"><span>[</span>83<span>]</span></a></sup> Students who complete the OCC requirements receive an OCC &quot;transcript&quot; and a green cord of distinction to wear at commencement.<sup id="cite_ref-Pitt_to_Offer_Students_Opportunity_to_Develop_Professional_Skills_Through_Extracurricular_Experiences_in_a_New_Program:_Outside_the_Classroom_Curriculum_to_be_implemented_this_fall_84-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pitt_to_Offer_Students_Opportunity_to_Develop_Professional_Skills_Through_Extracurricular_Experiences_in_a_New_Program:_Outside_the_Classroom_Curriculum_to_be_implemented_this_fall-84"><span>[</span>84<span>]</span></a></sup></p> 
     <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="International_studies">International studies</span><span class="mw-editsection">[<a href="/w/index.php?title=University_of_Pittsburgh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: International studies">edit</a>]</span></h3> 
     <div class="thumb tright"> 
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a href="/wiki/File:Indianroom2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Indianroom2.jpg/220px-Indianroom2.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Indianroom2.jpg/330px-Indianroom2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Indianroom2.jpg/440px-Indianroom2.jpg 2x" /></a> 
       <div class="thumbcaption"> 
        <div class="magnify">
         <a href="/wiki/File:Indianroom2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"><img src="//bits.wikimedia.org/static-1.22wmf8/skins/common/images/magnify-clip.png" width="15" height="11" alt="" /></a>
        </div> The Indian Classroom, one of 29 
        <a href="/wiki/Nationality_Rooms" title="Nationality Rooms">Nationality Rooms</a> in the Cathedral of Learning
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <p>Pitt’s history of commitment to international education is illustrated by its unique collection of 29 <a href="/wiki/Nationality_Rooms" title="Nationality Rooms">Nationality Rooms</a> on the first and third floors of the <a href="/wiki/Cathedral_of_Learning" title="Cathedral of Learning">Cathedral of Learning</a>. As a further demonstration of this commitment, Pitt is one of the country’s leading producers of both Fulbright scholars and Peace Corps volunteers<sup id="cite_ref-chancellor-2006_74-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-chancellor-2006-74"><span>[</span>74<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-University_Center_for_International_Studies_.28UCIS.29_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-University_Center_for_International_Studies_.28UCIS.29-85"><span>[</span>85<span>]</span></a></sup> and one of less than 20 American universities to claim five or more area studies programs that have been competitively designated as National Resource Centers by the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Education" title="United States Department of Education">U.S. Department of Education</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-pitt-fall-07_86-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pitt-fall-07-86"><span>[</span>86<span>]</span></a></sup></p> 
     <p>Pitt's National Resource Centers include Asian, European, Latin American, Russian and East European, and Global studies,<sup id="cite_ref-ritchie_87-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ritchie-87"><span>[</span>87<span>]</span></a></sup> as well as Pitt's International Business Center.<sup id="cite_ref-pitt-fall-07_86-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pitt-fall-07-86"><span>[</span>86<span>]</span></a></sup> In addition, Pitt's Asian Studies Center has been awarded status as a <a href="/wiki/Confucius_Institute" title="Confucius Institute">Confucius Institute</a> by the Chinese Ministry of Education.<sup id="cite_ref-Chinese_Ministry_of_Education_Awards_University_of_Pittsburgh_First_Confucius_Institute_in_Pennsylvania_88-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chinese_Ministry_of_Education_Awards_University_of_Pittsburgh_First_Confucius_Institute_in_Pennsylvania-88"><span>[</span>88<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Confucius_Institute_at_the_University_of_Pittsburgh_89-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Confucius_Institute_at_the_University_of_Pittsburgh-89"><span>[</span>89<span>]</span></a></sup> Further, Pitt is home to one of just ten European Union Centers of Excellence in the U.S., funded by the <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a>.<sup class="Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2012)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p> 
     <p>The <a href="/wiki/University_of_Pittsburgh_Center_for_International_Studies" title="University of Pittsburgh Center for International Studies">University Center for International Studies</a> (UCIS) coordinates international education curricula, centers on topical specializations in international studies, and the centers for area studies, including the National Resource Centers, among existing faculty and departments throughout the university. It does not itself give degrees but awards certificates of attainment to degree candidates in the University's schools and also operates certificate programs in African Studies (undergraduate) and in Global Studies (undergraduate &amp; graduate).<sup id="cite_ref-about-ucis_90-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-about-ucis-90"><span>[</span>90<span>]</span></a></sup> UCIS also operates the Study Abroad Office,<sup id="cite_ref-Study_Abroad_Office_91-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Study_Abroad_Office-91"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup> Nationality Rooms and Intercultural Exchange Programs.<sup id="cite_ref-about_nationality_rooms_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-about_nationality_rooms-92"><span>[</span>92<span>]</span></a></sup></p> 
     <p>Pitt's study abroad program, under the auspices of UCIS, helps to facilitate student study in over a hundred different countries, and oversees a variety of programs including the Panther Programs, which are course taught abroad that have been developed and are accompanied by faculty of the university; two-way exchange agreements with foreign institutions; and Pitt-recognized, third-party exchange programs.<sup id="cite_ref-Study_Abroad_Program_Options_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Study_Abroad_Program_Options-93"><span>[</span>93<span>]</span></a></sup> The university also offers several study abroad scholarships, including those through the Nationality Rooms program.<sup id="cite_ref-Scholarships_for_Study_Abroad_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scholarships_for_Study_Abroad-94"><span>[</span>94<span>]</span></a></sup> In addition, following the decision to end a 24-year sponsorship of the <a href="/wiki/Semester_at_Sea" title="Semester at Sea">Semester at Sea</a> program due to academic, administrative and safety concerns,<sup id="cite_ref-Provost_explains_decision_to_drop_Semester_at_Sea_95-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Provost_explains_decision_to_drop_Semester_at_Sea-95"><span>[</span>95<span>]</span></a></sup> Pitt has created a Multi-region Academic Program (PittMAP) that involves international travel, accompanied by university faculty, to three different continents for the comparative study of one of six rotating global study themes.<sup id="cite_ref-Pitt_Map_Program_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pitt_Map_Program-96"><span>[</span>96<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-robinet_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-robinet-97"><span>[</span>97<span>]</span></a></sup></p> 
     <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rankings">Rankings</span><span class="mw-editsection">[<a href="/w/index.php?title=University_of_Pittsburgh&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Rankings">edit</a>]</span></h3>
